The platform is user-friendly, cloud-based, and accessible from anywhere, making it easy to manage campaigns efficiently. Moreover, Awin consistently introduces numerous and attractive new advertisers through the network. The platform allows for the rapid creation of suitable affiliate links, and all data and statistics can be accessed through the API. Awin is continuously developing its platform, making it a highly reliable partner for us. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">However, Awin has small areas that could use improvement. The lack of direct customer support via email or phone can be a drawback, especially for issues requiring immediate attention.
</p><p class="formatted-text">The search function can be somewhat lacking, making it challenging to find specific advertiser. This can be a frustrating experience when trying to locate particular partners within the network. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-9894863 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Awin solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Awin effectively solves several key problems that affiliate marketers often face. One major issue is the need for a diverse range of advertisers to collaborate with, and Awin excels in providing a vast network of potential partners. This diversity helps in finding the right match for different marketing strategies and target audiences. Additionally, the clear and concise reporting/tracking and the API significantly simplify our workflow. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div The platform's intuitive interface makes finding and joining relevant programs straightforward. I particularly appreciate the seamless integration process and the ease of accessing a wide variety of high-quality advertisers. The dashboard is user-friendly, providing clear insights and comprehensive analytics that help me optimize my campaigns effectively. 
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Moreover, we are thrilled with the dedicated account managers who consistently go above and beyond to support us. Their expert guidance and personalized assistance have been invaluable in helping us maximize our affiliate marketing success. Overall, Awin has greatly enhanced our ability to manage and grow our affiliate marketing efforts with minimal hassle. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Awin?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The approval process for new publishers. Occasionally, it takes a long time to get accepted into programs, which can be frustrating and delays the start of potential campaigns. Speeding up this process would significantly enhance the user experience and help publishers begin their marketing efforts more efficiently. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-9912738 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Awin solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Earning money by redirecting customers to the right products! <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex In that time we've had issues with the implementation and commission structure, and we had to complain heavily about the lack of support from our dedicated person at AWIN before being moved to a new advisor who is much for efficient and useful for what we need. If you are on shopify the integration is not that easy to use. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8868067 </p><p class="formatted-text">Thank you for taking the time to share your positive experience with Awin. We're delighted to hear that you consider us the best platform, and we truly appreciate your kind words about our support team.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">We understand that uploading promotional materials can be challenging at times, and we appreciate your feedback. We're actively working on improving the user experience.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Thank you again for your glowing review and for choosing Awin. We value your partnership and look forward to continuing to exceed your expectations.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
